 However, there is good news for those who are looking to buy Hyundai Venue
 autokarindia kii report ke mutabik, is esayuvi kii aadhikarik booking 2 may, 2019 se shuru ho jaaegi
 As far as the price is concerned, it is expected that the price of this car can be kept from Rs 8 lakh to Rs 12 lakh (ex-showroom)
 is car ke fitures kii baat karen to isamen front dark krom gril, LED drls ke saath projector hedlamp, LED telolamp or projector tip fog lamps die gaye hai
 Apart from this, it will also get features such as air purifier, wireless charger, cruise control, rear AC vents, glow box cooling and electric sunroof
 sabase khaas baat ye rahegi ki is esayuvi main aapako 'bluelink'l connactivity technology kaa bhi saport milegaa
 It will get 33 connectivity features, out of which 10 features have been included especially for India
 yahaan 8-inch kaa tachascreen imphotonment system bhi graahakon ko milegaa
 Apart from all this, customers will also get two petrol and one diesel engine with this SUV

 com / stayxrgo6l 108 saal pehle germany main ek sandesh ko bottle main band kar samudr main chhod diya gaya tha

 1904 se 1906 ke bich uttari sagar main is bottle band sandesh ko samudr main phenkaa gaya tha jo ab jaakar germany ke amarum bich par ek mahila ko mila he
 It is written on a postcard sealed in a bottle, whoever gets this bottle, please send it to the Marine Biological Association (MBA) of the United Kingdom

 bider 1939 se 1945 tak emb ke adhyaksh bhi rahe

 Every year, there are reports of devastation caused by earthquake incidents all over the world
 aapke pairon ke tale se jameen khinchne vaale ye kampan badi badi imaaraten ukhaad phenkate hai
 But, in a particular region of the Himalayas that covers the region from Nepal to Afghanistan, here the highest earthquake incidents occur
 kya aapako pataa he ki kyon himalay ke in khaas rigen main hi bukamp kyon aata he
 According to scientific analysis, the part around the Himalayas is known as the Indian Plate
 vahiin duusari ore afghanistan he, isaki ore kaa hissaa uresia plate ke rup main pahachaanaa jaataa he
 The third part associated with these two is the Arab and African plate which is connected to many countries
 himalay ke aasapaas ke in ilaakon main aksar bukamp aane kii vajah hi ye hoti he ki jab ye plates ek-duusare ke kshetra main ghusane kii koshish karte hai to ye ek duusare se ragad khaati hai
 This causes a large amount of energy from the friction of these plates
 isi tej gharshan yaa friction se upar kii dharti dolane lagati he
 Not only this, many times the earth around the area explodes, sometimes for weeks and sometimes for several months, this energy is passed out intermittently and this is why earthquakes keep happening
 jaane - kya kahati he 2012 main chhapi ye research:-research ke mutabik himalay ke sabase mukhya yani kendriya hisse main richter scale par 8 se 8
 There have been many earthquakes of magnitude 5 - large earthquakes have caused deep cracks in this entire area, especially in the year 1934 earthquakes changed the map around the Himalayas
 -1934 main aae bukamp ne to sataha par 150 kilometre lambii daraar bana di thi, jo aaj bhi puri tarah bhari nahin ja saki he
 In the opinion of Himalayan mountaineers made of similar earthquakes, the Indian plate lying miles down in the earth is moving towards the Eurasian plate at the rate of 45 mm per year
 inke khisakane se ye donon plates aapas main ragad rahi hai
 The result of this friction has been the formation of the Himalayas
 jaise jaise in donon plates ke bich gharshan badha, dharti thodaa sa khiski or parvat banataa rahaa
 Today the Himalayas are lifesaving for many countries, but scientists also say that if the friction between these two plates increases, then this mountain can also become the cause of great destruction in the coming time
 sabhapati ne donon hi netaaon ko apni baton ko sabit karne or tathyon ko sadan main dene kaa aadesh diya
